The game and its variants are popular in many countries and under various names.\r\n\r\nParchisi originated in India by the 6th century. \r\n\r\nEach player rolls the die; the highest roller begins the game. The game and its variations are popular in many countries and under various names.\r\n\r\nHow to play Ludo Table :\r\nEach player gets to choose tokens of one of the four colors (green, yellow, red or blue).
